                <h2 class="heading feed-heading--underline feed-heading--large">Wilfried Bony joins Swansea</h2>
            </a>
            <time class="timestamp feed-timestamp" data-mcfc-time="1504221240000" datetime="2017-08-31T23:14:00.000Z">Thursday, August 31, 2017 10:14 PM</time>
        </div>
        <a href="/news/first-team/first-team-news/2017/august/wilfried-bony-man-city-swansea-transfer-news" class="faux-link-block--link" tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true">Wilfried Bony joins Swansea</a>
    </article>
</div>                                                    <div class="news--articles--secondary cf" data-scroll-item data-news-secondary-items>
